Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery is only useful for lead poisoning, except when it comes to the method known as "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the methods that we have described in sections, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary for you to make four cauterizations around the anus, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the intestines, and one at the buttocks under the spine, and one place on the breasts; and let the cauterizations be well close to the spinal notch of the hips.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les .ij. ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After that, leave the cautery in place to purify for a long time and don't stop treating the patient after the cautery; and then recovery would speed up and both treatments (the cautery and the other remedies) would work together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the belly is like the one we have shown before; and the one for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what was illustrated earlier.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the joints
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the fingers swell in someone who is hypoplastic, and are full of yellow bile, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the first and second knuckle; and lift your hand with the cautery without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much in the form, thus it would get rid of the yellow bile and perform according to this shape with the cauterization:
Aprés fai sus .ij. jambes .ij. cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After applying two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the heel; and make the cauterizations along the length, one in front of the knee cap and the other behind, halfway down the leg; and let the cauterizations last for a long time without treating them until the bile comes out; after you have treated all the other treatments as we have said.
de la menoison	on memory
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai .i. grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et .iiij. cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout .i. cautere clavile subtil, et .ij. cauteres sus les hainches.	When it comes to the problem of abdominal pain due to cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and retaining virtues in the stomach and intestines are compromised and not functioning properly, they cannot be treated by conventional methods; you notice that the patient is suffering significantly and with considerable strength, so apply one large gastric cautery according to what was discussed previously or the gastric cautery, with the circulating cautery; and four additional cauteries around the mouth of finer material in each spot. Apply one fine clavicle cautery and four more on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see that the moisture is abundant and the patient suffering, then apply a cautery to the knife point, and one cautery on each hand, and two small ones on the stomach near the large intestine. For the treatment benefits when there's good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	regarding the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorroids are or have their foundation, or one or more and are old, they contain large cold and moist putrefied humors. If it is treated as we have said in divisions and does not benefit, then do cauterizations: III over the spine on the back, that which is all beyond the spot where the stomach meets with the small intestine a little by little in triangularizing, and I cauterization just below the navel II inches; and if you think that the stomach has cooled down and the food does not cook, and one sees swelling of the belly, then to the belly perform a large cauterization as was previously said, and another over the liver, and another on the spleen with all the cauterizations being used. Leave the cauterizing for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the inflammation known as 'thelul'
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble .i. raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou .ij., et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you apply the hot iron, if it seems to be .i. razed, and then place all of it on fire over this iron; keep your hand there until the heat reaches the beginning of the vein from which the blood comes; do this once or twice, and if there are multiple parts, cauterize each one as we have said; after using beneficial ointments while they are still good; and if you use a large heated iron to treat, it will provide greater assistance.
de plaie mal curee	from improperly treated wounds
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot tolerate surgery or opening a wound, as we will explain in its appropriate section, if such sickness occurs that can only be cured through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If no cure comes about, and it worsens with gangrene and infected moisture, if you must test fully with a delicate attempt, and be sure that you know the full extent of the attempt in terms of how much perfection it has.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cautery until it seems ready, and applying it to the fistula according to how deeply the attempt has entered, and continue the cautery as long as the putrid and infected parts are burned away; one time, or two, or three times, according to your need. And be careful not to burn nerves that are present, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the bladder or the intestine, be aware of these points, and do not perform this outside the body. Do it only in the abdominal cavity. Remember that this is not a minor surgery. After treating the wound until it heals, and if there are pus points and oozing matter for a long time, then you know that the pus point has been completely healed. And if the matter is not solidified, you should know that there is still pus in the body, and the bone at its root is corrupted; do this as one of these we will tell you about in the body.
de la maladie des reins	On the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra .iij. cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When stomach pain comes from the kidneys and large windiness affect a woman's body, then it is necessary for you to apply the cautery on both sides of the kidneys and with the wrist cautery as we have previously mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauteries in line, and they would provide more assistance.
de la vessie	From the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et .i. a destre et .i. a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais .i. cautere defuers le dos, ou .ij. se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is weak and moist due to cold, so that patients retain urine, then instruct for a cautery on the lower part of the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, and one on each side, both right and left. Each cautery should be as long as the width of a finger; and do one in front of the back or two if needed; and let the cauteries be round following the form mentioned beforehand.
de la marris	Regarding the treatment for Marosis
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice .iij. cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et .ij. cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers (likely referring to menstrual blood) are corrupted with delayed passage; and when they come, there's great pain: then it should be done that three cauterizations be performed inside the vaginal orifice, as we have said or for bladder cautery treatment, and two cauterizations at the back; and let the cauterizations be round, as we have said.
de la hainche	From the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a .i. cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moistors descend to the thigh bone, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that one leg is longer than the other when measured together; and you find the joints at their separation points, then it should be that you cauterize the skin on the thigh bone like one fire cautery resembling a circle, and mark before the joint where the bone turns, so that the bone is within the circle; and let the cauterizations be as those from which we have cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai .iij. cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if these cauterizations are not present, make three large olive-shaped cauterizations instead, and let the cauterizations be as perfect as all the others; and treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	The pain of the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain occurs in the buttock area, it is due to cold and moisture. The patient needs treatment for this as we have discussed earlier on division, and if the cure does not work, the disease is old: therefore, you should cleanse the body of large, thick humor with foul-smelling pills or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After you perform the cautery; and the method of the cautery is according to two ways: that is to say together with heated medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery has several methods, among which one is like this: you apply three triangular cauterizations according to this shape, and make them of good depth and large, with the space between each cautery being as wide as two fingers, and they should be olive-shaped; no middle cautery is made in the center of the hipbone, because there are four following this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that when cauterizing with the circular cautery as we have mentioned before regarding the dislocation of the buttocks; but do it in such a manner that the circles encompass all the buttock area, and all parts around the knee are burnt.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used in sciatica, when pain stays in the hip and doesn't reach up to the thigh or down to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations there where the disease says the pain holds them back, and one above the ankle four times, on the left side a little bit; and let the surgical blade make these cauterizations, and burn away the thickness of the heel; and if the disease feels that the pain extends up to half way down or close to the knee, then cauterize where they feel the pain three points or four at the cauterization marked 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if more work is needed, then do so; and if the pain seems to be spreading from the knee towards the thigh, apply cutler's or circular cauterization there, and ensure good care in all your cauterizations that you don't leave any part untouched, burning nerves and major arteries, and that you do not cause more harm and constriction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen several cases where cauterization was done on the ankle up to the knee, and they left them until the leg became completely swollen, and even the feet, which were pierced and corrupted entirely.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach treatment that led to death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are concentrated in two parts together, make a cautery on one part and another, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise man spoke about the cautery of the hipbone, as it is described here, make one such iron and have it at the head also as big as a snail's shell, or somewhat smaller, and have it with joints, and from each joint to another there should be an interval equal to the size of a pea; and let the joints be in two parts, and they should resemble knots, and each one should have a well-made iron boss; this is its form.
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois .i. cautere reont et lou laisse .iij. jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it's entirely red and gives off steam, then place it on the sore hipbone, and twist it towards the healthy side; and apply this cautery once for each rod and leave it there for three days; and afterwards, make a bandage of butter, and let the wound be open for as long as necessary; after oil treatment until it heals.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use very little of this type of cautery due to the fear of his patients, and there are few who use it; however, this is a good type of cautery which can be endured, and leaves no marks.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauterizing instruments of medicine consist in making an implement with joints where the edge of the door descends, and it can be made of steel or iron, being long on one side, and at its height there are two knots, each having the size equivalent to a button; they should have a forward edge and above, and they join together according to this form.
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing on the hip bone of the lying patient under his side without any injury to the sound part, and quickly place your hand mostly on the hip bone; afterwards pour between the two circles of the hot awl heated in the flame for a moment, and leave it for an hour. Allow the patient to endure the heat and burn from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For there is also burning like that of fire; and when the burnings have passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip gently upwards, and leave it thus for three days. Then apply butter until that which is black from the scalding fades away; and let it be for three more days until putrefaction sets in; and after this would be the last aid following the treatment of ointments as long as he is sound.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, you must make the cautery mark it as far as possible according to what you did at the hip joint; and this is how one uses hot cauteries, and I have written about them concerning the rectification of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicksilver and powdered sulfur, in equal amounts of each, grind them together, and place the mixture in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Let it have the small thorn that a razor point might be able to enter; and place this mixture in another well-weighed pot, and add quicksilver and sulfur gently on top, until there is twice as much liquid above the powders as you will have taken with your hand; and leave it like this until the essence comes out in oil and dregs or the pot is weighed down. Then take all this essence, and pour it over sulfur and quicksilver just as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And thus it will be very useful and administered in movements of medical work and in other member's cauteries For it performs a work akin to fire, and with other medicines one does well to cauterize the hip such as turpentine and anacardium oil mixed with soap, all these things combined together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment for someone who was cured of hip pain and sciatic nerve pain, and much delight, and says that no other treatment was done, and that they were healed in one go once this treatment was performed, and they bathed as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And instructs to do it in this manner that you take fresh and dry litargy (a mineral) powder, and mix it thoroughly with a little fat, then apply it on the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain lies, and bind it. Leave it for three hours until the pain no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make them enter into a bath until their body becomes somewhat aroused, and make them rest on the bed, and the pain will go away completely and they shall be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	Know that no one should use such medical instruments as a cautery, unless after the removal of pus or bodily fluids.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides states that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's urine, it helps a little; and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take grease and mix it with old oil, then apply it to the depression that is between the thumb on the foot and the one called the heel bone.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking dried goat urine, apply it to the fire until it becomes ashes and then mix it with grease. Place this mixture on the fabric and let it harden completely before removing it. Repeat this process several times until you think that the treatment should reach up to the hip, and until the pain is alleviated; this type of cautery is called "goat urine cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by impact or from percussion or due to excessive evacuation, or due to any appearance of cold matter spread out, none of these appearances are worth cauterizations, for it is akin to what comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne .v. cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai .iij. cauteres ou .iiij. au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary that after the maladies have been emptied of rotten pills or other appearances, one should be performed on the back, where the pain resides, three lines marked by an incision, and in each line from 5 to more cauterizations according to the strength and quantity the maladies can endure; and let the cauterizations be done as with the cautery called "points"; and if you see fit, perform 3 or 4 cauterizations at the midpoint of the clavile cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often befalls the young children, and at its beginning it is such that they become pale when they stand up, and fear; and you find in the last spinal cord of the back and within us the appearance that comes upon other spinal cords.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe its cure, if you apply it with a blood cautery in the form described like this.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cautery burns each segment of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, cauterize around the spine along the length of the cautery for two or three lines, and make sure the points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the treatment as long as it remains healthy according to what we have said, and be cautious not to use the cautery in a state of illness near nerve areas.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain in joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When joint pain arises from moisture spreading throughout each limb, and when the pain affects the foot, it's referred to as 'gout' properly, and when it's due to cold reasons and can be treated with medicines alone, it should be cured using cauterization in this manner: make a cauterization around the joint of the foot, and let the olive oil cauterizer look like this:

And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, you should cauterize at each knee with three or four on each part of the oil area; and if you need more, you may do so, but don't let your hand go beyond until the keur's skin is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend as far as the knees and behind, then he should be treated with the cautery that we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, then make cuts between the second and third lines; and if there remains any pain in the arms, then make cuts on each joint and around the hair of the hand; and if the pains come up to the elbows or shoulders, then cauterize each part, and take good care of the patient and administer remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you give him good care and cleanse the pus, he will be cured with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of the uterus
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When rupture occurs in anger, and the bowels descend into the crotch which is new, it must be that when you see them being cured, do not let him eat that day; and use things that relax the stomach so that his intestines descend from his belly; after make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to shave his pubic hair until the bowels are repaired, then take it with your fingers, and test for any movement over the rupture on the bone under the knife, and at all a sign that is similar to half of a circle above the navel; then heat up the cautery as described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and discharges scabs.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the pus from its place; and let the attendants cut her hand so it doesn't turn back; and treat his thighs well to the patient, and put a cloth and a bandage on his thighs, and another on his buttocks where he cuts his hands; then apply the cautery to your sign on all your hand, and yours straight until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it on the first try, start again another time until you reach the bone; and watch carefully so that no pus flows when you do the cautery, not to burn him; and let the patient not die or any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach to the bone at the cautery, your procedures are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it must be that the cauteries of children are subtle according to their size, and those of large people also as big as their measure; after three days, apply a butter ointment on the lesion with the fire cautery until the scab is removed; afterwards apply other remedies until they heal properly, and let the patient lie for forty days under his back so that the wound is well sealed; and it must be that these exercises are exhausted for a long time, so that blisters do not come out when he wants to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wants to stand up, let him wear a well-made bandage and leave it on for another forty days; and have good rest, let him work lightly and guard against too much drinking and eating, and too much shouting; and when he does this lesson properly, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after this about the treatment of trimming in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Regarding the rupture of the stomach

des porrelz qui vienent as piez	The text "des porrelz qui vienent as piez" translates to "the stones that come towards the bones" in English. This seems to describe a medical issue related to stones or deposits moving towards bone structures, which could be a description of gallstones, kidney stones, or other similar conditions in medieval medical terminology.
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Sometimes, when a wound opens up and produces a disease which is called "constriction" according to our understanding, it results in a large bulging thing that causes pain on the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatments for this disease do so according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This means understanding fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	The fire cautery requires you to heat until it glows like a goose feather and should be made of good iron at the size that allows piercing from every side. Make sure there are fine margins. Once heated fully on the nail, twist your hand around the nail immediately as soon as it touches the tip; leave him in this position for three days until it begins to fester; then apply an ointment of crushed wild vinegar mixed with oil over night and leave this ointment for the whole duration. The nail will come out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cleanse it with a greasy ointment until the wound is healed.

And if they are converted through the belly and many times occur in hands and in feet, it is necessary for you to bring in hot cautery of water; and be as follows: take one of an arable stick or iron, or a goose feather, and place on the nail and its root. This refers to removing warts. Place the stick so that it burns completely around, then put a bit of hot water, and keep your hand well fixed, pressing your hand as you twist the stick until the margin of the stick reaches to the root of the nail; then find the deep passage of hot water until it touches the root; and let the patient endure the slight burning from hot water for an hour; then leave him like this, and all roots will be uprooted completely.

li cure dou trembler	The treatment involves shaking.

des pustules puans	pus-filled sores
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No appearance from behind the surface of the body, or pus-filled boils, that come from large decayed materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	When they become visible from the boil's surface that come from large decayed materials, it is necessary at first when they appear to apply a fine fire cauterizer: a willow stick's tip with its point seized in fire, or from a long root of rhubarb, or using a lentil-shaped cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And each time they are cauterized in the beginning when they become visible following this manner, and they cannot grow pus forwards but it removes the excess from which they come, and they are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times great hemorrhages of the artery occur from where it is cut in the wound that reaches to the opposite side, or at incision of the abscess, or with the cautery on the limb, and similar situations; and it is a very grievous thing to occlude.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren .i., ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And yet, when this happens to any person, if you quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein and hold it firmly until the pulse becomes quiet under your finger, and no more drops escape; then heat several olive oil cauteries of various sizes until they are all red. Then take one, or a larger or smaller according to the size of the wound and the location where the artery is located, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your index finger, and keep the cautery there until the pulse becomes still again.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cauteries are off the fire, then quickly take another one of the cauteries that are on the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des .iiij. manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And never stop doing this one after the other until the bone is fully healed; and be careful not to burn the nerve that's nearby, and that no harm comes upon the patient; and know that when there is a break in an artery, it can't be mended very well by itself when the artery is large, unless done through one of the four ways we've mentioned: by cautery, or extraction if not already treated, or with strong stringing, or with medicines placed which have power to mend blood; and then tie and hold in place.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will provide for the mending by tightly binding with cloths or by putting heat sources on, or other similar things, if they do not benefit unless so prescribed.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they have no medicine or remedy at hand, should apply their finger on the wound site as we said before, and spread it well until the wound and the vein are mended upon it; and do not move his hand but keep it moist with cold water often till it becomes very cold until the bone is frozen, swollen, and mended. And perform cautery and medicine preparations for what needs them.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for surgery
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have explained in the first chapter all diseases where it is necessary to use a fire cautery or hot medicine, and we discussed their causes, instruments, and forms. I put that chapter up until the foot, and I will proceed through this chapter using the same path as what seems easier for those who want it.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And as I begin this one, you should know that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first about the cauteries, so it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	And few people come for treatment in any way.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from those who despair so much with their illness that they die lightly due to the madness they find in their disease, and the severity of their wickedness; one must have fear from these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are those who give their meaning and say: "Wait, I am sick"; and the illness is troublesome.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not right that you consent to those who come to you in this manner, but place more care on your honor than on your greed, and do not rashly but wisely follow those whom you are certain of, and can take advice from; use prediction and indication in the treatment of your patients for whose welfare it is meant; and this will help you acquire good reputation, glory, and lasting memory. And this will assist you to attain a noble reputation, glory, and enduring memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, Our Lords give us good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have arranged this chapter in devising by chapters, according to what is before or the chapter on cauteries, which I have devised from head to feet, because you will find it more easily of that which you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	at the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this disease comes very often to children at birth, and when the mother constrains the head of the child too tightly; and sometimes it occurs due to a response reason that one does not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease in anyone other than children, and among all those I have observed, their death hastened; for which reason it seems to me that it would be better to divide the work of this chapter into these cures.
Et je vis .i. enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com .ij. nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child of this, the shoulder was full of water, and the head swelled each day so much that it could no longer bear it; and believed to such moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled under the bone near the elbow, between the chest and the bone; and the muscles are like these when moisture is between the chest and the bone, and abscesses are small, that you cut in the middle of the head a wide crack; and let it be so long as two fists, as long as the moisture flows; and see this form of the syphilitic:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, make two cuts in a manner like an X, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief .iij. fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see that the edges of the head are opened from each part, and the water spurts out when you press it from your hand inside, and this is not relieved: then you must make three cuts in the middle of the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after making the incision, remove all moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After holding the suture cuts and powder openings, and applying wine and oil, leave them like this until the fifth day; then remove the stitches, treating the wound with dressings and ointments, and allow the head to heal equally. Finally, have the patient eat dried meat from a source with little moisture until the limb is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of making an incision is that you look at where the opening of the abscess is, and place the hot iron; for it is never in front; it's never behind; not to the right; nor to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, make the cut where the abscess opens, and place the hot iron, and perform the incision according to what you are able; and be careful not to damage an artery; watch for a flow of blood, so that the patient dies due to bleeding and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	On cautery of fire commands the diseased person to let their hair grow long and even; and if they poke at their origin, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to anyone that a disease is called "catarrh" with the eyes or at the bottom, and this disease is old, and the medicine treatment does not help, then the last resort procedure should be the cautery, using which one would cut off the two major arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, once the patient can see properly; after rubbing their eyes with a harsh cloth until the arteries are visible, then extract the eye from all of the socket; then check where the veins lie and ensure that both sides are equal to each other and behind the ears, and they have started to heal; then mark the sides with an iron tool, rub them with a sharp cutlass blade for two parts, until the edges reach the bone, and this must be done so as not to damage the surrounding tissue.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, pinch the pus near the artery and the vein above, cutting also as one inch through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let the blood flow out continuously from high up.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open upon feeling it, you should measure the size of the space in three fingers. Then press and go until you reach the bone; and that which needs to be expelled from the blood is six c/, and by chance a little more or less according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains up against the bone precisely like syphilis, if there are no signs suggesting an abscess beneath, then tighten the wound, bandage it, and apply ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	In the treatment of a fire cautery, instruct the patient to let their hairs grow long and evenly; if they prick at their base, hold them still so they do not move until they fully grow.
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	As the old age comes with and experiences acute inflammation and congestion, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and lower back areas from past illnesses and similar issues; medicine treatment for these is done through methods of medical cure techniques. Yet, none of these treatments are effective, so we remove the arteries in the temples and apply fire cautery, as we have detailed.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method for extracting them is such that the patient feels behind their temples, and listens to the artery which opens up at the temple, as it opens well through its pulsation, and responds only in some people who are too cold; if it does respond, then cool the neck of certain cloths, then rub it with a rough cloth, and raise the head under hot water until the artery appears clearly. Then take the sponge that is shaped like this:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then lightly strip the skin until you feel the artery, then lift it up with forceps and remove well the layers which are from each part; and if the artery is thin, if you twist it at the tip of the nail, then cut that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it isn't sewn, neither will escape without all pain everywhere.
Et trai dou sanc des .vj. c/, jusc’a .iij.; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en .ij. leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les .ij. liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And remove the blood from two to three; and if the artery is large, it should be tied with two threads of a strong silk thread, so that corruption does not occur in front of the healing of the wound, nor in subsequent bleeding; then cut off the excess between the two threads at this moment. And if you see, then apply the cautery gently until you reach the bone as long as the joints are cut; and this is the completed work, if the patient doesn't have fever and has warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	And the cauterization helps to finish off infections: because it provides more assistance against infections.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de .ij. pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	In order for the removal of arteries, fill the area with old cotton and place it on well-made gauze; when you separate them, apply dry medicines that produce heat and gauze until they are clean; and should you cut into the artery as you work, quickly use a cautery or fill the area with vitriol and press your hand against it so that the wound is sealed; and if you do not have this present, place ice on the area instead until the wound is frozen, then rinse with cold water while keeping the wound from moving; and treat it as necessary. The one who moves faster during artery extraction when using a cautery should cauterize the blood vessel by cutting it in half across, but ensure that the cuts are deep enough to retain more of its heat for longer periods.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too tight, they retain less of their heat.
Et doit avoir entre les .ij. coutelz .i. doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les .ij. leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en .ij. leus; et soient esloigniet entre les .ij. chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And must have a gap of one large finger between the two knives, and then when you prepare to apply them both at once, and place the hot iron until it reaches the bone, and cut the blood vessel in two; and keep them apart from each other with the shoulder joints because there is no welding effect throughout this cautery technique; and this is how a cautery should be formed:
des larmes	Of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes are flowing from veins above the testicle of the head of strength, and no medical remedy benefits, and you see the reddening action of the patient, and feel or front pulsation as if gasping; and at places they are tenacious and moist such that the hair of papers falls, and the papers heat up, and burn from the intensity of the tears, then it requires this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And they called the old "wound healer", and if you treat the person with this illness, make the hairs grow where he has hair or on his forehead, then make three cuts evenly across the forehead according to its length; and let one cut be as two doves along the whole forehead in such a way that it goes forward until it touches at the nose tip, and the other ones are each two doves above each rib under the skin. And avoid cutting the arteries which are above each rib under the skin; keep your hand away from the continuation of the two jaws, and let each wound have the size of three doves across; and prepare a piece of sponge and some cloths for wiping off blood, then use the sharp spatula blade formed out of two parts to cut.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les .ij. fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	From the incision that is made below the temple up to the second incision; and burn all the kerf that is between the two gaps throughout the entire sinus located above the bone. Then cut further along from the middle incision up to the other second, and then remove this pus-filled space.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If there is a tool placed in the first gap which is called 'cultellaire', and it has very sharp edges on one side, but not so on the other, it forms this:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And make the cut towards the soft flesh at the knee, and the cut go towards the bone at the leg, and the blade until it feel in the middle crack.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer; et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris; puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne; et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And make cuts to all veins that descend from the head as needles until the incision is continuous up to the one that opens at the knee, and then do the same thing in the middle cut until the other opening; and then drain equal blood, express the leg for the blood taken; then put in each crack a tent of old cotton, and place on wet cloths with vinegar and oil and aspen bark, and ensure that abscesses don't appear; and on the third day untie the bandage, and give large doses of water tea, then apply a cure of ointment basil with olive oil, and other cures used for wounds, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees; et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue; adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	When there is a sudden onset of thick expectoration and you see the eyes withered and small, and weakening of vision, and burnt paper; and the hair falls out, and one sweats in fullness from fever, and the patient shivers, and the body is racked by fevers. Then know through these incidents that those substances and this mucus come from many veins, and the wet treatment applied, if it is correct, then this is how it should be.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And indeed, you instruct the patient behind their forehead, then make a great incision through the forehead, and another quite wide just below it.

de l’estoupement des oreilles	On the cauterization of ears

de l’estoupement des oreilles	On the cauterization of ears

de la char des papieres	Of the wax of papers

de la gresle	Of the gravel
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz; li ovraiges est telz: pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir; fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope. If you can't cover it without piercing a bit of the paper, as long as it doesn't harm the patient; and if there's a large tear, stitch it up with one seam, and treat until it heals; and if it's small, don't apply too much force, because the ointment will heal it quickly and stimulate tissue growth.

de la graisse des eulz	From the grease of the ulcers
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz; et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil. des poilz des papieres	"Des poilz des papieres" translates to "Paper hair" in English. However, this phrase doesn't seem to make much sense contextually and could potentially be a typo or an error in the translation. If it's referring to paper made from hair, then it might mean something like "hair-based paper". The precise meaning would depend on the broader context of its use within the text.
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz; et est li cure selonc .iiij. manieres: ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	When hair grows out of place other than its natural position and ages, they harm the eyes and bring on ailments such as familiar infections and degenerations of paper-like tissues, as well as albugine disease, all because these causes lead to destruction of the eyes; and one must cure according to four methods: or with a fire cautery combined, or by using medicine in accordance with what is stated before or concerning the chapter on cautery, and this can be done either through incision and suturing or by ligation, depending upon which I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre; s’elle est convertie, c’est boin; se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout .i. fil desus; et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai .i. fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur; puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit; puis estrai .i. fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	It is necessary for you to place the eye's main part in its health. Then turn the paper of the eye with your left hand; if it turns, that is good. If not, then insert one needle through both layers at once. And do this either inside or outside the paper edge where hair grows from these hairs. Then pull two threads upwards across all the paper and turn them on a seam. Then cut along part under the paper, under those hairs in place, from the large tear up to the small; then remove one thread, and insert between the paper a little cotton tent, and on top of the paper make a figure like an asterisk, as if it were the leaf of a myrtle tree.
